</code></div></div></pre><ol start="3"><li><strong>Create a content script (<code>content.js</code>):</strong></li></ol><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>js</span><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-js">chrome.<span class="hljs-property">runtime</span>.<span class="hljs-property">onMessage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">addListener</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params">request, sender, sendResponse</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (request.<span class="hljs-property">action</span> === <span class="hljs-string">"getDOM"</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Access the DOM of the current website</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> domContent = <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-property">documentElement</span>.<span class="hljs-property">outerHTML</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Send the DOM content back to the background script</span>
    chrome.<span class="hljs-property">runtime</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">sendMessage</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">action</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"sendDOM"</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">content</span>: domContent });
  }
});
</code></div></div></pre><ol start="4"><li><strong>Create a popup HTML file (<code>popup.html</code>):</strong></li></ol><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>html</span><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-html"><span class="hljs-meta">&lt;!DOCTYPE <span class="hljs-keyword">html</span>&gt;</span>

[.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5 overflow-x-auto"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>Certainly! Here's a breakdown of the workflow for the given browser extension:</p><ol><li><p><strong>Manifest File (<code>manifest.json</code>):</strong></p><ul><li>This file provides essential information about the extension, such as its name, version, description, and permissions.</li><li><code>"manifest_version": 2</code> indicates that the extension is using manifest version 2.</li><li><code>"background"</code> specifies the background script (<code>background.js</code>) that runs in the background and handles browser events.</li><li><code>"content_scripts"</code> specifies the content script (<code>content.js</code>) that is injected into matching web pages.</li><li><code>"browser_action"</code> defines a button in the browser toolbar and a popup (<code>popup.html</code>) that appears when the button is clicked.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Background Script (<code>background.js</code>):</strong></p><ul><li>Listens for the browser action button click using <code>chrome.browserAction.onClicked</code>.</li><li>Sends a message to the content script when the button is clicked, triggering the content script to access the DOM of the current page.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Content Script (<code>content.js</code>):</strong></p><ul><li>Listens for messages from the background script using <code>chrome.runtime.onMessage</code>.</li><li>When it receives a "getDOM" message, it accesses the DOM of the current webpage (<code>document.documentElement.outerHTML</code>).</li><li>Sends the DOM content back to the background script using <code>chrome.runtime.sendMessage</code>.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Popup HTML (<code>popup.html</code>):</strong></p><ul><li>Defines the HTML structure of the popup.</li><li>Includes a button (<code>#getDOMButton</code>) to trigger the DOM retrieval and a <code>&lt;pre&gt;</code> element (<code>#domContent</code>) to display the retrieved DOM content.</li><li>Links a script (<code>popup.js</code>) for handling popup behavior.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Popup Script (<code>popup.js</code>):</strong></p><ul><li>Listens for button clicks in the popup using <code>addEventListener</code>.</li><li>When the "Get DOM" button is clicked, it queries the active tab using <code>chrome.tabs.query</code> and sends a "getDOM" message to the content script.</li><li>Listens for messages from the content script using <code>chrome.runtime.onMessage</code>.</li><li>When it receives a "sendDOM" message, it updates the content of the <code>&lt;pre&gt;</code> element with the retrieved DOM content.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Icon (<code>icon.png</code>):</strong></p><ul><li>A small icon representing the extension, which appears in the browser toolbar.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Loading the Extension:</strong></p><ul><li>The extension is loaded into the browser by going to <code>chrome://extensions/</code>, enabling "Developer mode," and clicking "Load unpacked" to select the extension directory.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Usage:</strong></p><ul><li>Clicking the extension's button in the browser toolbar opens the popup.</li><li>Clicking the "Get DOM" button in the popup triggers the content script to access the DOM of the currently active webpage.</li><li>The retrieved DOM content is displayed in the popup.</li></ul></li></ol><p>This workflow allows the extension to interact with the DOM of the active webpage and display the content in a popup when the user clicks the extension's button.</p></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex justify-start gap-3 empty:hidden"><div class="text-gray-400 flex self-end lg:self-center justify-center lg:justify-start mt-0 -ml-1 visible"><span provided example, the interaction with the DOM is initiated when the user clicks the "Get DOM" button in the popup. The relevant function for initiating the process is the event listener attached to this button in the <code>popup.js</code> script.</p><p>Here is the relevant part of <code>popup.js</code>:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>js</span><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-js"><span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getElementById</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"getDOMButton"</span>).<span class="hljs-title function_">addEventListener</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"click"</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  chrome.<span class="hljs-property">tabs</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">query</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">active</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">currentWindow</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">true</span> }, <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params">tabs</span>) {

  });
});
</code></div></div></pre><p>In this code snippet:</p><ul><li><code>document.getElementById("getDOMButton").addEventListener("click", function() {...}</code> sets up an event listener for the "click" event on the button with the ID "getDOMButton" in the popup HTML.</li><li><code>chrome.tabs.query({ active: true, currentWindow: true }, function(tabs) {...}</code> queries the active tab in the current window.</li><li><code>chrome.tabs.sendMessage(tabs[0].id, { action: "getDOM" });</code> sends a message to the content script in the active tab, triggering it to access the DOM and send it back to the extension.</li></ul><p>If you want to initiate the DOM retrieval programmatically from another context (e.g., background script), you can use the same <code>chrome.tabs.sendMessage</code> method with the appropriate tab ID and message payload.</p><p>For example, in the <code>background.js</code> script, you could initiate the DOM retrieval by calling:</p><pre><div class="bg-black   chrome.<span class="hljs-property">tabs</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">sendMessage</span>(tabs[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>].<span class="hljs-property">id</span>, { <span class="hljs-attr">action</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"getDOM"</span> });
});
</code></div></div></pre><p>This assumes that you have a valid reason to trigger the DOM retrieval from the background script. The example architecture was designed with user interaction in mind to ensure that the extension only accesses the DOM when the user explicitly clicks the "Get DOM" button.</p></div></div></div><div To achieve that, you would need to modify both the content script (<code>content.js</code>) and the background script (<code>background.js</code>). Here's an updated version of the code to accomplish this:</p><ol><li><strong>Update <code>content.js</code>:</strong></li></ol><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>js</span><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-js">chrome.<span class="hljs-property">runtime</span>.<span class="hljs-property">onMessage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">addListener</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params">request, sender, sendResponse</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (request.<span class="hljs-property">action</span> === <span class="hljs-string">"getDOM"</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Access the DOM of the current website</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> domContent = <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-property">documentElement</span>.<span class="hljs-property">outerHTML</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Get the URL of the active tab</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> tabUrl = <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-property">location</span>.<span class="hljs-property">href</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Create an object with url and data</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> result = {
      <span class="hljs-attr">url</span>: tabUrl,
      <span class="hljs-attr">data</span>: domContent
    };

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Send the result back to the background script</span>
    chrome.<span class="hljs-property">runtime</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">sendMessage</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">action</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"sendDOM"</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">result</span>: result });
  }
});
</code></div></div></pre><ol start="2"><li><strong>Update <code>background.js</code>:</strong></li></ol><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>js</span><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-js">chrome.<span class="hljs-property">browserAction</span>.<span class="hljs-property">onClicked</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">addListener</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params">tab</span>) {
  chrome.<span class="hljs-property">tabs</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">sendMessage</span>(tab.<span class="hljs-property">id</span>, { <span class="hljs-attr">action</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"getDOM"</span> });
});

chrome.<span class="hljs-property">runtime</span>.<span class="hljs-property">onMessage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">addListener</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params">request, sender, sendResponse</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (request.<span class="hljs-property">action</span> === <span class="hljs-string">"sendDOM"</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Access the result object containing url and data</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> result = request.<span class="hljs-property">result</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Now 'result' contains {url: "...", data: "..."}</span>
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"URL:"</span>, result.<span class="hljs-property">url</span>);
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Data:"</span>, result.<span class="hljs-property">data</span>);
  }
});
</code></div></div></pre><p>Now, when you click the "Get DOM" button in the popup, the content script will not only retrieve the DOM but also the URL of the active tab. The content script then sends an object containing both the URL and the DOM content back to the background script. The background script logs the URL and the data to the console, but you can modify it to perform any further processing as needed.</p></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex justify-start gap-3 empty:hidden"><div class="text-gray-400 flex self-end lg:self-center justify-center lg:justify-start mt-0 -ml-1 visible"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 categorize elements based on their tags in the DOM and create an object, you can modify the content script (<code>content.js</code>) to filter out container elements and categorize the remaining elements. Here's an example of how you can achieve this:</p><ol><li><strong>Update <code>content.js</code>:</strong></li></ol><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>js</span><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-js">chrome.<span class="hljs-property">runtime</span>.<span class="hljs-property">onMessage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">addListener</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params">request, sender, sendResponse</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (request.<span class="hljs-property">action</span> === <span class="hljs-string">"getDOM"</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Access the DOM of the current website</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> domContent = <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-property">documentElement</span>.<span class="hljs-property">outerHTML</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Get the URL of the active tab</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> tabUrl = <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-property">location</span>.<span class="hljs-property">href</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Create an object with url and categorized elements</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> result = {
      <span class="hljs-attr">url</span>: tabUrl,
      <span class="hljs-attr">elements</span>: <span class="hljs-title function_">categorizeElements</span>(<span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-property">body</span>)
    };

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Send the result back to the background script</span>
    chrome.<span class="hljs-property">runtime</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">sendMessage</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">action</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"sendDOM"</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">result</span>: result });
  }
});

<span class="hljs-comment">// Function to categorize elements based on their tags</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">categorizeElements</span>(<span class="hljs-params">element</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> categorizedElements = {};

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Traverse all child nodes of the given element</span>
  element.<span class="hljs-property">childNodes</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">forEach</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params">node</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (node.<span class="hljs-property">nodeType</span> === <span class="hljs-number">1</span>) { <span class="hljs-comment">// Check if it's an element node</span>
      <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> tagName = node.<span class="hljs-property">tagName</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">toLowerCase</span>();

      <span class="hljs-comment">// Ignore container elements, you can customize this list</span>
      <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> ignoredContainerElements = [<span class="hljs-string">"div"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"section"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"article"</span>];

      <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!ignoredContainerElements.<span class="hljs-title function_">includes</span>(tagName)) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Add or update the count for the specific tag</span>
        categorizedElements[tagName] = (categorizedElements[tagName] || <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) + <span class="hljs-number">1</span>;

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Recursively categorize child elements</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> childCategories = <span class="hljs-title function_">categorizeElements</span>(node);
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Merge the child categories into the main object</span>
        <span class="hljs-title class_">Object</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">assign</span>(categorizedElements, childCategories);
      }
    }
  });

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> categorizedElements;
}
</code></div></div></pre><p>In this updated code:</p><ul><li>The <code>categorizeElements</code> function is introduced to traverse the DOM tree, categorize elements based on their tags, and ignore certain container elements.</li><li>The <code>categorizedElements</code> object is created and updated for each encountered tag, and the count of each tag is incremented.</li><li>Container elements specified in the <code>ignoredContainerElements</code> array are excluded from the categorization.</li></ul><p>Now, when you click the "Get DOM" button in the popup, the content script will categorize the elements based on their tags, excluding specified container elements, and send the result back to the background script. The result object will contain the URL and the categorized elements. Adjust the <code>ignoredContainerElements</code> array as needed based on the container elements you want to exclude from categorization.</p></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex justify-start gap-3 [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5 overflow-x-auto"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>Certainly, I understand. You want to create an object where each tag corresponds to an array containing the text content of all the elements with that tag. Here's how you can modify the <code>categorizeElements</code> function in <code>content.js</code> to achieve this:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>js</span><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-js">chrome.<span class="hljs-property">runtime</span>.<span class="hljs-property">onMessage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">addListener</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params">request, sender, sendResponse</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (request.<span class="hljs-property">action</span> === <span class="hljs-string">"getDOM"</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Access the DOM of the current website</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> domContent = <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-property">documentElement</span>.<span class="hljs-property">outerHTML</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Get the URL of the active tab</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> tabUrl = <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-property">location</span>.<span class="hljs-property">href</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Create an object with url and categorized elements</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> result = {
      <span class="hljs-attr">url</span>: tabUrl,
      <span class="hljs-attr">elements</span>: <span class="hljs-title function_">categorizeElements</span>(<span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-property">body</span>)
    };

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Send the result back to the background script</span>
    chrome.<span class="hljs-property">runtime</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">sendMessage</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">action</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"sendDOM"</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">result</span>: result });
  }
});

<span class="hljs-comment">// Function to categorize elements based on their tags</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">categorizeElements</span>(<span class="hljs-params">element</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> categorizedElements = {};

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Traverse all child nodes of the given element</span>
  element.<span class="hljs-property">childNodes</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">forEach</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params">node</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (node.<span class="hljs-property">nodeType</span> === <span class="hljs-number">1</span>) { <span class="hljs-comment">// Check if it's an element node</span>
      <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> tagName = node.<span class="hljs-property">tagName</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">toLowerCase</span>();

      <span class="hljs-comment">// Ignore container elements, you can customize this list</span>
      <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> ignoredContainerElements = [<span class="hljs-string">"div"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"section"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"article"</span>];

      <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!ignoredContainerElements.<span class="hljs-title function_">includes</span>(tagName)) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Get the text content of the element</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> textContent = node.<span class="hljs-property">textContent</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">trim</span>();

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Add the text content to the array for the specific tag</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!categorizedElements[tagName]) {
          categorizedElements[tagName] = [textContent];
        } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
          categorizedElements[tagName].<span class="hljs-title function_">push</span>(textContent);
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Recursively categorize child elements</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> childCategories = <span class="hljs-title function_">categorizeElements</span>(node);
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Merge the child categories into the main object</span>
        <span class="hljs-title class_">Object</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">assign</span>(categorizedElements, childCategories);
      }
    }
  });

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> categorizedElements;
}
</code></div></div></pre><p>In this modified version:</p><ul><li>Instead of counting occurrences, it stores an array of text content for each tag.</li><li>If a tag has not been encountered before, it creates a new array for that tag in the <code>categorizedElements</code> object. If the tag has been encountered before, it appends the text content to the existing array.</li></ul><p>This way, the resulting <code>categorizedElements</code> object will have tag names as keys, and each key will map to an array containing the text content of the corresponding elements.</p></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex justify-start gap-3 empty:hidden"><div class="text-gray-400 flex dark"><p><code>document.body</code> and <code>document.documentElement.outerHTML</code> represent different parts of the HTML document.</p><ol><li><p><strong><code>document.body</code>:</strong></p><ul><li><code>document.body</code> refers to the <code>&lt;body&gt;</code> element of the HTML document.</li><li>The <code>&lt;body&gt;</code> element typically contains the main content of the HTML page, such as text, images, links, and other elements.</li><li>Accessing <code>document.body</code> allows you to </code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong><code>document.documentElement.outerHTML</code>:</strong></p><ul><li><code>document.documentElement</code> refers to the root element of the HTML document, which is usually the <code>&lt;html&gt;</code> element.</li><li><code>outerHTML</code> is a property that returns the HTML serialization of the entire element, including its start tag, attributes, content, and end tag.</li><li><code>document.documentElement.outerHTML</code> provides the entire HTML content of the document, including both the <code>&lt;head&gt;</code> and <code>&lt;body&gt;</code> sections.</li></ul><p>Example:</p><pre><div class="bg-black rounded-md"><div class="flex items-center relative text-gray-200 bg-gray-800 dark:bg-token-surface-primary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>javascript</span><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M12 4C10.8954 4 10 4.89543 10 6H14C14 4.89543 13.1046 4 12 4ZM8.53513 4C9.22675 2.8044 10.5194 2 12 2C13.4806 2 14.7733 2.8044 15.4649 4H17C18.6569 4 20 5.34315 20 7V19C20 20.6569 18.6569 22 17 22H7C5.34315 22 4 20.6569 4 19V7C4 5.34315 5.34315 4 7 4H8.53513ZM8 6H7C6.44772 6 6 6.44772 6 7V19C6 19.5523 6.44772 20 7 20H17C17.5523 20 18 19.5523 18 19V7C18 6.44772 17.5523 6 17 6H16C16 7.10457 15.1046 8 14 8H10C8.89543 8 8 7.10457 8 6Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div><div class="p-4 overflow-y-auto"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> fullHTML = <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-property">documentElement</span>.<span class="hljs-property">outerHTML</span>;

class="">Content.js

chrome.runtime.onMessage.addListener(function(request, sender, sendResponse) {
    if (request.action === "getDOM") {
      // Access the DOM of the current website
      var domContent = document.documentElement.outerHTML;
  
      // Get the URL of the active tab
      var tabUrl = window.location.href;
  
      // Create an object with url and categorized elements
      var result = {
        url: tabUrl,
        elements: categorizeElements(document.body)
      };
  
      // Send the result back to the background script
      chrome.runtime.sendMessage({ action: "sendDOM", result: result });
    }
  });
  
  // Function to categorize elements based on their tags
  function categorizeElements(element) {
    var categorizedElements = {};
  
    // Traverse all child nodes of the given element
    element.childNodes.forEach(function(node) {
      if (node.nodeType === 1) { // Check if it's an element node
        var tagName = node.tagName.toLowerCase();
  
        // Ignore container elements, you can customize this list
        var ignoredContainerElements = ["div", "section", "article"];
  
        if (!ignoredContainerElements.includes(tagName)) {
          // Get the text content of the element
          var textContent = node.textContent.trim();
  
          // Add the text content to the array for the specific tag
          if (!categorizedElements[tagName]) {
            categorizedElements[tagName] = [textContent];
          } else {
            categorizedElements[tagName].push(textContent);
          }
  
          // Recursively categorize child elements
          var childCategories = categorizeElements(node);
          // Merge the child categories into the main object
          Object.assign(categorizedElements, childCategories);
        }
      }
    });
  
    return categorizedElements;
  }

content.js:

chrome.runtime.onMessage.addListener(function(request, sender, sendResponse) {
    if (request.action === "getDOM") {
      // Access the DOM of the current website
      var domContent = document.documentElement.outerHTML;
  
      // Get the URL of the active tab
      var tabUrl = window.location.href;
  
      // Create an object with url and data
      var result = {
        url: tabUrl,
        data: domContent
      };
  
      // Send the result back to the background script
      chrome.runtime.sendMessage({ action: "sendDOM", result: result });
    }
  });

		console.log("Data:", result.data);
    }
});
